## HOW TO USE THIS GUIDE

1. **Identify your query topic** — what subject, concept, or question?
2. **Scan the Section Directory below** — find the most relevant section(s)
3. **Check the Topic Cluster Tables** — find specific documents by topic cluster
4. **Use the Cross-Section Query Router** — for queries spanning multiple domains
5. **Go directly to the document** — open `[SectionLetter][##]_Name.md`

## RELIABILITY QUICK REFERENCE

| Tier | Meaning | Trust Level | Example |
|------|---------|-------------|---------|
| **1 — VERIFIED** | Peer-reviewed, primary texts, archaeological consensus | HIGH — cite directly | DNA double helix, Göbekli Tepe dating |
| **2 — CREDIBLE** | Academic, debated but supported | MEDIUM — cite with caveat | Sphinx water erosion, Orch-OR theory |
| **3 — SPECULATIVE** | Possible but unverified | LOW — present as hypothesis | Atlantis location, DNA-shamanism link |
| **4 — DUBIOUS** | No credible evidence | VERY LOW — present as rejected | Shapeshifting leaders, flat Earth |

**Source Confidence:** `[N/5]` = rating based on bibliography count. `[5/5]` = 21+ sources. `[4/5]` = 15-20. `[3/5]` = 11-14. `[2/5]` = 7-10. `[1/5]` = 1-6 sources.
